<script type="text/javascript">
      //
        function JOT_insertRelDate(timestamp, absTimeStr, isSiteLocale, dir) {
          var relTimeStr = JOT_formatRelativeToNow(timestamp, isSiteLocale);
          if (relTimeStr) {
            if (isSiteLocale) {
              document.write('<span timestamp="' + timestamp + '" issitelocale="' + isSiteLocale +
                '" title="' + absTimeStr + '" dir="' + dir + '">' + relTimeStr + '<' + '/span>');
            } else {
              document.write('<span timestamp="' + timestamp + '" title="' + absTimeStr +
              '" dir="' + dir + '">' + relTimeStr + '<' + '/span>');
            }
          } else {
            document.write(absTimeStr);
          }
        }
      //
      </script>

style="background-color:transparent;color:rgb(0,0,0);font-size:medium;line-height:normal"><font color="#000080" face="arial, sans-serif" size="4">Biography</font></b></p><hr style="color:rgb(0,0,0);font-size:13.3333px" /><font color="#000000" face="georgia, serif"><span style="font-size:15px;white-space:pre-wrap">Daibo Liu is currently a Yuelu Assistant Professor at the College of Computer Science and Electronic Engineering in Hunan University. He received the PhD degree from the College of Computer Science and Engineering in University of Electronic Science and Technology of China in 2018. He was a Visiting Research Fellow at the Department of Software in Tsinghua University from 2014 to 2016, and was a Visiting Student at Department of Electrical &amp; Computer Engineering in UW-Madison from 2016 to 2017. He joined in Hunan University as a faculty member in Mar., 2018. He leads the Networking and Smarting Sensing Systems research group </span></font><span style="background-color:transparent;color:rgb(0,0,0);font-family:georgia,serif;font-size:15px;white-space:pre-wrap">with Prof. </span><span style="background-color:transparent;color:rgb(0,0,0);font-family:georgia,serif">Hongbo Jiang</span><span style="font-size:15px;white-space:pre-wrap;color:rgb(0,0,0);font-family:georgia,serif;background-color:transparent">. His current research interests include <b>IoT systems and networks, edge computing, wireless and mobile computing</b>. </span></div><div style="line-height:16.6667px;border-style:none none solid;border-bottom-color:rgb(170,170,170);border-bottom-width:1pt;padding:0cm 0cm 2pt"><br /><p align="left" style="color:rgb(0,0,0);font-size:13.3333px;margin:8.4pt 0cm Liu</b>, Mengshu Hou. </span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size:13pt;font-family:Times New Roman"><a href="https://sites.google.com/site/dbliuuestc/" rel="nofollow"><b><font color="#000000">A novel method for multiple depot and open paths,Multiple Traveling Salesmen Problem</font></b></a></span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size:13.0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;color:black">, </span><span style="color:rgb(0,0,0);font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:17.3333px;background-color:transparent">In</span><span lang="EN-US" style="line-height:24pt;font-size:13pt;font-family:Times New Roman;background-color:transparent"><font color="#000000"> </font></span><span lang="EN-US" style="line-height:24pt;font-size:13pt;font-family:Times New Roman;color:black">IEEE SAMI 2013, Herlany, Slovakia, January
31 - Feburary 2, 2013. </span><span lang="EN-US" style="line-height:24pt;font-size:13pt;font-family:Times"><font color="#000000"> <u>[</u></font><u><a href="https://sites.google.com/site/dbliuuestc/" style="margin-bottom:12.0pt;margin-left:42.0pt;text-align:left;line-height:24.0pt;background:white"><br /></p><div style="color:rgb(0,0,0);font-size:13.3333px;line-height:16.6667px;border-style:none                       var loadTimer = window.jstiming.load;
                      loadTimer.tick("ol");
                      loadTimer["name"] = "load," + webspace.page.type + ",user_page";
                      window.jstiming.report(loadTimer, {}, 'https://gg.google.com/csi');
                    }
                  </script>

<script xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml" type="text/javascript" defer="true">
  //<![CDATA[
    // Decorate any fastUI buttons on the page with a class of 'goog-button'.
    if (webspace.user.hasWriteAccess) {
      JOT_decorateButtons();
    }

    // Fires delayed events.
    (function() {
      JOT_fullyLoaded = true;
      var delayedEvents = JOT_delayedEvents;
      for (var x = 0; x < delayedEvents.length; x++) {
        var event = delayedEvents[x];
        JOT_postEvent(event.eventName, event.eventSrc, event.payload);
      }
      JOT_delayedEvents = null;
      JOT_postEvent('pageLoaded');
    })();
  //]]>
</script>
